 agle dedh saalon main aise phone milane lag jaaenge
 Broadcom, the company that makes mobile phone chips, gave this information

 4ji technology apni purvavarti 3ji se paanch guna tej he lekin abhi is par chalane vaale handset mahange hai
 4G handset running in India is at least Rs 18,000 but most handsets are not less than Rs 40,000
 iske vipareet 3ji se las phone saste ho gaye hai or unki keemten 4,000 rupee se kam ho gai he

 ) a three-day mahamanthan will start in and out of Parliament from December 27 on the much-discussed Lokpal Bill
 samaadhaan is baat par nirbhar karegaa ki sansad ke bheetar satta paksh or vipaksh kis had tak saath aa pate hai or inhen teen din anna hajaare mumbai main anshan par baithenge
 On the other hand, BJP and Left parties have given notice to introduce amendments
 unhone lokapal or lokayukta vidheyak, 2011 main kuch sanshodhan prastaav rakhane kaa faisla kiya he
 Anna Hazare traveled six hours by road from his village Ralegan Siddhi to Mumbai and now he will sit on a hunger strike at MMRDA ground in Mumbai
 sarkaar ne team anna se vidheyak par sansad ke faisle kaa intjaar karne ko kaha he lekin hazaare ne mumbai ke mrdie maidan main anshan par baithne se ek din pehle apane rukh main kisi tarah kii narmi nahin aane kaa sanket dete hue kaha ki unki chaar maangon par samjhauta sambhav nahin he
 74-year-old Hazare, who is suffering from viral infection, also said he would go on a hunger strike amidst lack of health and claimed that his agitation was not against any person, party or party
 mumbai ke mrdie maidan main anna apane sahyogiyon ke saath rahenge to unke anya saathi dilli ke ramlila maidan main pradarshan karenge
 Increasing the problems of the government, the main opposition party BJP and Left parties have also announced that if the government did not agree on their suggestions, they will bring amendments on the bill

 itnaa hi nahin goa main party kaa khaataa bhi nahin khulaa or arvind kejariwal ke saare sipaahi goa ke chunavi samar main dher ho gaye
 After the Punjab election result, a big question arises that what will happen to the "AAP"? Arvind Kejriwal's national plans have suffered a setback due to the results of Punjab and Goa
 punjab ke baad arvind kejariwal kii najar narendra modi ke garh gujarat par thi jahaan isi saal disambar main chunaav hone hai

 agar punjab ke nateezon kaa asar dilli ke nigam chunaav par pada to yahaan bhi aam aadmi party ko jhatka lag saktaa he or phir arvind kejariwal kii lokapriyata par sawalia nishaan paidaa ho jayega

 anshan sthal ke baahar saikadon kii taadaad main log qatari lagaae khadey hai
 Ramdev staged at around 4
50 am in the morning amid the thunderous applause of his supporters
 unhone subah 5 se 7 baje ke bich samarthakon ko yogasana sikhaaya
 Along with his fast, the yoga guru is also running an Ashtanga yoga camp at Ramlila Maidan
 unhone subah 7 baje apana anshan shuru kiya or isi ke saath bharat mata kii jai or bhrashtachar mitaayenge, desh bachaayenge jaise naare lagane kii bhi shuruyaat ho gai
 Since 7 am, the process of singing bhajans is going on at Ramlila Maidan
 bhajan gane ke liye manch par sabhi saz bhi maujuud hai
 Ramdev sits on a 1,200 sqft platform built at a height of 12 feet with his close ones
 ramlila maidan ke baahar logon kii kareeb ek kilometre lambii qatari lagi he or log besabri se maidan ke andar pravesh paane kaa intjaar kar rahe hai
 However, Ramdev's supporters have to undergo a stringent security check before entering
 saikadon kii sankhya main badi teji se jute rahe logon kii bheed ke maddenjar dilli police ne ramlila maidan par kade suraksha intjaam kiye hai
 Commandos along with the policemen of Delhi Police are also holding the front
 suraksha ke maddenjar ramlila maidan main pravesh ke liye ek hi dwaar rakhaa gaya he, jahaan metal detector vaale daravaaje lagaaye gaye hai or logon kii do-do baar talaashi bhi lee ja rahi he
 Officials of Patanjali Yogpeeth and Bharat Swabhiman Trust claim that more than 50,000 people have gathered on the Ramlila grounds
 inamen se adhiktar haryana, uttar pradesh, uttarakhand or punjab se aae hai
 Ramdev told his supporters before starting the fast, nothing is impossible
 sab kuch sambhav he

 ramlila maidan main subah se hi mediakarmiyon kaa hujum umada hua he
 Volunteers are present at various places in the city to guide the people to the Ramlila grounds
 ve baba ke samarthakon ko anshan sthal tak jane kaa rasta bataa rahe hai
 Manoj Tiwari said, 'I don't have any problem with splattering, but it is not right to speak wrong about one's mother
 ' yah ghatana shanivaar ko bengal kii duusari pari ke aathven over ke dauraan hui jab manan sharma kii gend par parthasarathi bhattacharya out hokar pavilion laute
 Tiwari then came out to bat at number four, wearing a cap
 tiwari ne guard liya or vah strike lene ke liye taiyaar the, lekin unhone gendbaaj ko roka or dressing room se helmet mangavaya, kyonki duusare chor se tej gendbaaj gendbaaji kar rahaa tha
 Delhi players felt that this was a deliberate time-wasting strategy
 manan ne iske baad tiwari se bahes kii or unhone use apana kaam karne ko kaha
 Suddenly standing in the first slip, Gambhir came forward and he abused the Bengal captain, who responded
 dilli ke khilaadiyon ko laga ki yah jaanboojhkar samay barbaad karne kii ranneeti he
 Manan then argued with Tiwari and he asked him to do his work
 achaanak pehali slip main khadey gambhir aage aa gaye or unhone bengal ke captain ko apshabd kahe, jinhone iskaa jawaab diya
 a daughter is shot dead by a father in Naroli, UP
